[2018-04-06 15:13:43] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180401.MANUAL.41/4121/0811/20'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122F210'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-06 15:43:02] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180401.MANUAL.41/4121/1213/3267'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122F210'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )

[2018-04-06 15:44:43] Koreksi BCC STEP 41 : SELECT CASE
											WHEN NO_REKAP_BCC < 10
											THEN
												CONCAT('0',NO_REKAP_BCC)
											ELSE
												TO_CHAR(NO_REKAP_BCC)
											END
												AS NO_REKAP_BCC
											FROM (
								SELECT substr(NO_REKAP_BCC,-1)+1 NO_REKAP_BCC, rown
								  FROM (SELECT a.*, ROWNUM rown
										  FROM (  SELECT *
													FROM t_detail_rencana_panen
												   WHERE ID_RENCANA =
															'20180401.MANUAL.41/4121/0811/20'
														 AND id_ba_afd_blok = '4122F210'
												ORDER BY NO_REKAP_BCC DESC) a)
								 WHERE rown = 1
								 )
